create schema medicwall;

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
create table city
(
    id        integer not null
        constraint city_pkey
            primary key,
    name      varchar,
    ibge_code integer,
    uf        varchar
);

alter table city
    owner to postgres;

create table role
(
    id   serial  not null
        constraint roles_pk
            primary key,
    name varchar not null
);

comment on table role is 'Identificadores de role';

alter table role
    owner to postgres;

create unique index roles_id_uindex
    on role (id);

create unique index roles_name_uindex
    on role (name);

create table expertise
(
    id   serial  not null
        constraint expertise_pk
            primary key,
    name varchar not null
);

comment on table expertise is 'expertises medicas';

alter table expertise
    owner to postgres;

create unique index expertise_id_uindex
    on expertise (id);

create unique index expertise_name_uindex
    on expertise (name);

create table adress
(
    id            serial  not null
        constraint adress_pk
            primary key,
    fk_city       integer not null
        constraint adress_city_fk
            references city,
    nbhood        varchar(40),
    street        varchar(40),
    num           integer,
    complement    varchar(100),
    postalcode    integer,
    register_date date    not null
);

comment on table adress is 'endereço do usuário';

alter table adress
    owner to postgres;

create unique index adress_id_uindex
    on adress (id);

create table contact
(
    id            serial  not null
        constraint contact_pk
            primary key,
    name          varchar not null,
    fone          varchar(16),
    fone2         varchar(16),
    name_alt      varchar,
    fone_alt      varchar(16),
    register_date date    not null
);

comment on table contact is 'contact de usuário';

alter table contact
    owner to postgres;

create unique index contact_id_uindex
    on contact (id);

create table document
(
    id  serial  not null
        constraint document_pk
            primary key,
    cpf varchar not null,
    rg  varchar not null,
    crm varchar
);

comment on table document is 'documentação do usuário';

alter table document
    owner to postgres;

create unique index document_id_uindex
    on document (id);

create unique index document_cpf_uindex
    on document (cpf);

create unique index document_rg_uindex
    on document (rg);

create table conf_doctor
(
    id            serial  not null
        constraint conf_medic_pk
            primary key,
    fk_espec      integer not null
        constraint conf_medic_expertise_id_fk
            references expertise,
    start_time    time    not null,
    end_time      time    not null,
    consult_time  integer not null,
    price         integer not null,
    register_date date    not null
);

comment on table conf_doctor is 'Configurações do médico';

alter table conf_doctor
    owner to postgres;

create unique index conf_medic_id_uindex
    on conf_doctor (id);

create table conf_patient
(
    id            serial           not null
        constraint conf_patient_pk
            primary key,
    weight        double precision not null,
    height        integer          not null,
    allergies     varchar,
    register_date date
);

comment on table conf_patient is 'Configurações do paciente';

alter table conf_patient
    owner to postgres;

create unique index conf_patient_id_uindex
    on conf_patient (id);

create table "user"
(
    id              serial  not null
        constraint user_pk
            primary key,
    role_id         integer not null
        constraint user_roles_id_fk
            references role,
    email           varchar not null,
    password        varchar not null,
    name            varchar not null,
    birthdate       date    not null,
    active          boolean not null,
    fk_contact      integer not null
        constraint user_contact_fk
            references contact,
    fk_document     integer not null
        constraint user_document_fk
            references document,
    fk_adress       integer not null
        constraint user_adress_fk
            references adress,
    fk_confpaciente integer
        constraint user_conf_patient_id_fk
            references conf_patient,
    fk_confmedico   integer
        constraint user_conf_medic_fk
            references conf_doctor,
    register_date   date    not null
);

comment on table "user" is 'Login e fk''s';

alter table "user"
    owner to postgres;

create unique index user_id_uindex
    on "user" (id);

create unique index user_email_uindex
    on "user" (email);

create unique index user_fk_confmedico_uindex
    on "user" (fk_confmedico);

create unique index user_fk_confpaciente_uindex
    on "user" (fk_confpaciente);

create unique index user_fk_contact_uindex
    on "user" (fk_contact);

create unique index user_fk_document_uindex
    on "user" (fk_document);

create unique index user_fk_adress_uindex
    on "user" (fk_adress);

create unique index user_name_uindex
    on "user" (name);

create table schedule
(
    id               serial  not null
        constraint schedule_pk
            primary key,
    doctor_id        integer not null
        constraint schedule_user_doctor_id_fk
            references "user",
    patient_id       integer not null
        constraint schedule_user_patient_id_fk
            references "user",
    start_time       time    not null,
    end_time         time    not null,
    price            money,
    canceled         boolean,
    canceled_reason  varchar,
    appointment_date date    not null,
    register_date    date    not null,
    observation      text
);

alter table schedule
    owner to postgres;

create unique index schedule_id_uindex
    on schedule (id);

create table docsec_rel
(
    id        serial not null
        constraint docsec_rel_pk
            primary key,
    sec_id    integer
        constraint docsec_rel_user_sec_id_fk
            references "user",
    doctor_id integer
        constraint docsec_rel_user_doc_id_fk
            references "user"
);

alter table docsec_rel
    owner to postgres;

create unique index docsec_rel_id_uindex
    on docsec_rel (id);
